In 994 北府宰相兼領樞密使 and soon after also 北院樞密使, elevated to rank 大丞相 and made Prince of Qi. At that time held power over whole Liao army. In 1011.4.11 died. (遼史/卷15)
1401693 = { #韓德威 Han Dewei, courtesy name 普鄰 Pulin. Fifth son of Han Kuangsi according to 惕隱司秦王帳空寧敵烈太保墓誌, third son according to 遼史. Between 969 and 979 made an official in Shangjing and prefect of Ruzhou 儒州防禦使, 北院宣徽使. In 983 because his father died, succeeded temporarily 西南招討使. Later this year five tribes of Tanguts raided southwest, Han Dewei Pacified them. Was made 領知突呂不部、迭剌部糾軍, pacified 稍古葛, and was made officially 西南招討使. In 986 together with Tigin Yelü Shanpu defeated Yang Ye. In 988 made 開府儀同三司, 政事令、門下平章事. Because Chengyi in Shanxi fell his command over troops was removed. In 992 Li Jiqian appeased Song, so Han Dewei led an expedition against Xi Xia and plundered Lingzhou. In 996 once again struck at Tanguts. Died the same year at the age of 55.

1401741 = { #耶律恕 Yelü Ru, Khitan name 耨里 Nouli. Member of Han household according to 金史. Due to lack of futher data on the parenthood, I'll make him a son of Abu. He liked reading books. Due to his knowledge of both Khitan scripts was early given a post. In 1122 Tianzuo escaped west and Liao fell. In 3rd month Ru surrendered to Jin along with Yelü Gaoba and was made a general under the command of Wanyan Loushi. Together with Marshal Wanyan Zonghan they invaded Song, Ru led the vanguard. In 1133 he took part in the battle of Hesheng Plain under the command of Wanyan Zongbi. Next year he took part in the battle of Xianran pass. Due to his skillful command of troops he was recommended to the post of the deputy prefect of Taiyuan and Zhending by Wanyan Zongpu. Later made 行台兵部侍郎、尚書左司郎中. After the enthronment of Wanyan Liang he was made a 沁南軍節度使 and 工部尚書. In 1150 安國軍節度使. In 1153 參知政事. In 1154 prefect of Xingzhong. In 1156 retired and made a prince of Guangping. The same year he died.
